32  /**
33   * Exhaustive serialization tests for all the HTML5 DTOs.
34   */
35  @SuppressWarnings({})
36  class Html5_ComboRoundTripTest extends ComboRoundTripTest_Base {
37  
38  	private static final B btag = b("bbb");
39  
40  	private static A a2(Object ref, Object...children) {
41  		return HtmlBuilder.a(ref, children);
42  	}
43  
44  	private static <T> ComboRoundTrip_Tester.Builder<T> tester(int index, String label, Type type, T bean) {
45  		return ComboRoundTrip_Tester.create(index, label, type, ()->bean);
46  	}
47  
48  	private static ComboRoundTrip_Tester<?>[] TESTERS = {
49  		tester(1, "A", A.class, a2("http://foo", "bar"))
50  			.json("{_type:'a',a:{href:'http://foo'},c:['bar']}")
51  			.jsonT("{t:'a',a:{href:'http://foo'},c:['bar']}")
52  			.jsonR("{\n\t_type: 'a',\n\ta: {\n\t\thref: 'http://foo'\n\t},\n\tc: [\n\t\t'bar'\n\t]\n}")
53  			.xml("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
54  			.xmlT("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
55  			.xmlR("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>\n")
56  			.xmlNs("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
57  			.html("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
58  			.htmlT("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
59  			.htmlR("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>\n")
60  			.uon("(_type=a,a=(href=http://foo),c=@(bar))")
61  			.uonT("(t=a,a=(href=http://foo),c=@(bar))")
62  			.uonR("(\n\t_type=a,\n\ta=(\n\t\thref=http://foo\n\t),\n\tc=@(\n\t\tbar\n\t)\n)")
63  			.urlEnc("_type=a&a=(href=http://foo)&c=@(bar)")
64  			.urlEncT("t=a&a=(href=http://foo)&c=@(bar)")
65  			.urlEncR("_type=a\n&a=(\n\thref=http://foo\n)\n&c=@(\n\tbar\n)")
66  			.msgPack("83A55F74797065A161A16181A468726566AA687474703A2F2F666F6FA16391A3626172")
67  			.msgPackT("83A174A161A16181A468726566AA687474703A2F2F666F6FA16391A3626172")
